If you are the first one to join, you would be assigned the drawer for the first round. You would be given a random word. While \"Paint Balling\", you can aim with your gaze and air tap to shoot paintballs.\r\n\r\nBefore teleporting in HoloLens, make sure the panel shows \"Teleport On\".
